name:Xâ€iâ€aâ€oâ€dâ€iâ€aâ€nâ€zâ€iâ€yâ€oâ€uâ€hâ€aâ€oâ€dâ€iâ€aâ€nâ€zâ€i

msg:It is a very good hotel

I often go out to play with my children and have stayed in many family hotels. This time I returned to my grandparentsâ€™ house in Weihai and took a boat to Yantai to stay overnight. After choosing a hotel for a long time, I found this five-star hotel with no bad reviews. I originally only chose hotels in the group chain, but suddenly I was curious. Mainly, it fully meets my requirements

Before checking in, I called to confirm and learned that I was directly upgraded to a parent-child room with my baby. The room is very large and newly decorated. The swimming pool is a seawater swimming pool and the gym also meets basic needs. There is also a mini children's playground with a laundry room and a microwave. Children's bed rails are also provided. The second hotel I encountered had a fence fixed to the bed with nails. Across the road is the sea. The sand is super fine and clean. I even think the experience this season is better than Sanya. I didnâ€™t bring sand digging tools and the front desk gave me a set for my baby.

The most important thing is that the hotel gave me the impression that the service was timely and sincere from the moment I parked the car. The concierge helped with luggage and guided me. After checking in at the front desk, I took him directly into the room and took a look at what was missing. It was brought to me right away. Any employee I encountered when I got lost in the hotel was kind and helpful. Returning to the room is very friendly to children. As long as any request is reasonable but not excessive, the hotel will basically meet it immediately.

There are few places to eat near the hotel, and takeout is more convenient. If you drive, itâ€™s beautiful to play along the coastline.

The only thing that I think can be improved is the breakfast. The variety of breakfast is very rich. The beef noodles with tofu are delicious. There is also sushi, but some ingredients may not be so fresh due to the off-season. The bread and pasta are also a bit hard. Some dishes are not replenished in time. But the overall experience is very good. I just hope that it will be more perfect when I come again next time.

In short, I will recommend it to my friends. I will also take the time to take my children to stay for a few more days. It is worth visiting again.
